See it as the agri-food system \"serious game\", based on collective intelligence and extremely educational because it allows you to learn a lot in a very short time, whether you're just curious or already knowledgeable.\nIt is also an opportunity to meet other people interested in the subject of the sustainability of our food, and to discover an effective tool to raise awareness and catalyze transformative action around you.\nAgenda & Practical Info\n  Workshop language : English.\n  Group introduction\nReconstruction of the Agri'Food Collage\nDebrief\nShare actions ideas\n  Recommended age: 16 and above.\nThis workshop will be held online via videoconference, and we'll be using a web-based visual collaboration tool. Quelles sont leurs cons\u00e9quences ?\nActions (30 min) : choix d\u2019une action individuelle et une action collective pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable et anticipation des difficult\u00e9s/freins qui pourraient \u00eatre rencontr\u00e9s\nD\u00e9brief (15 min) : retours sur l\u2019atelier, derniers conseils, quelle suite donner \u00e0 l\u2019atelier, ...\nCroyez-nous, \u00e7a passe (tr\u00e8s) vite !\nInfos pratiques\nMat\u00e9riel\nVous aurez simplement besoin d\u2019un ordinateur, d\u2019un micro et d\u2019une connexion internet suffisante pour pouvoir \u00e9changer avec les autres participant.e.s. Quelles sont leurs cons\u00e9quences ?\nActions (30 min) : choix d\u2019une action individuelle et une action collective pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable et anticipation des difficult\u00e9s/freins qui pourraient \u00eatre rencontr\u00e9s\nD\u00e9brief (15 min) : retours sur l\u2019atelier, derniers conseils, quelle suite donner \u00e0 l\u2019atelier, ...\nCroyez-nous, \u00e7a passe (tr\u00e8s) vite !\nInfos pratiques\nMat\u00e9riel\nVous aurez simplement besoin d\u2019un ordinateur, d\u2019un micro et d\u2019une connexion internet suffisante pour pouvoir \u00e9changer avec les autres participant.e.s.     "description": "4 pm to 7 pm Paris time\n  Check the time in your local time zone here\n    Facilitator: Marco BUSCEMI\n  Textiles are everywhere! In our clothing, furniture, toys and even computers! But how much do you really know about them? What exactly are our textiles made from? How sustainable are they, really? How far do our clothes travel before we buy them? Where do they go once they are donated?\n  This collaborative workshop illustrates the complexities and impacts (social and ecological) of the textile industry by using clothing as a case study. You will create the production chain of textiles, learn about the industry\u2019s impact, and then work together to find solutions and actions you can take.\n  This workshop is inspired by the pedagogy of the Climate Fresk (an interactive workshop that teaches the IPCC Climate report). Experience this unique way of learning, if you are new to the Fresk universe of workshops. Launched in 2021, Textiles UnTangled has been enjoyed by over 600 participants.\n  You will learn:\n  1. Materials 101 - What fabrics should I choose!?!\n2. The life cycle of textiles, from raw materials to end of life\n3. Textile industry impacts on the planet and on humans.\n4. How to think critically of claims made by companies & organizations about their sustainability\n5. Notions of circular economy, systems view thinking, and human centered solutions\n6. Actions that can be taken on a collective, business, and individual level\nAll while working together and having fun!\n  Our main sources: Ellen MacArthur Foundation, Preferred Textiles Report, OXFAM, Fashion Revolution and ADEME.\n  What participants have said:\n  \"This game is a fun, civic-minded and inclusive way to think about our relationship to clothing. Some companies who have played: Vestiaire Collective, Deloitte, Givenchy, Promod, Caroll and Minelli, Balzac, and Electrolux. For a private session you can contact: greendonut.info@gmail.com\n  Who is this by?\n  Textiles UnTangled game workshop (Textile Collage) was created by the volunteers at Green Donut. Created in France in 2019, Green Donut is an association whose mission is to promote the donut economics model by Kate Raworth (a society prospering within environmental and social limits) via their serious games and actions in the community. They are professionals, experts and concerned citizens of many backgrounds. While based in France, they have diverse backgrounds and welcome members from other countries.\n  Their website (in french only for now) with all their events including our Fresque de D\u00e9chets (Waste Collage = French only): http://greendonut.org\n  Commitment and Cancellation\n  This workshop is a small group workshop (max 8 participants) that needs a minimum to fully capitalise on our collective intelligence. If you must cancel, please do so a week before. Request a refund via Billetweb and it will be granted, minus the Evenbrite fees. If cancelled within a week, please let us know. You are welcome to transfer the ticket to someone else. You can notify us at greendonut.info@gmail.com. Thanks in advance.\n    Now let\u2019s learn about textiles to change the world together!\n   ",

What impacts do our consumption and waste generation have on those resources and on the planet in general?\nHow can I contribute to reducing those impacts in my daily life? How can companies evolve their business models?\nTo discover the answers to these and many other questions, come and take part in a workshop of the Circular Economy Collage. The workshop covers topics such as climate change, biodiversity loss, resource scarcity and pollution generated by human activities and enables you to identify concrete courses of action!\nAbout the workshop\nThe Circular Economy Collage is a stimulating, group-based workshop founded on scientific information, which enables participants to grasp the limits of our existing global \u201clinear\u201d economy and understand the opportunities offered by the circular economy. Inspired by the Climate Fresk, the workshop will allow you to understand the issues surrounding our use of natural resources and our generation and treatment of waste as well as other impacts caused by human activities. The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",

If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. The workshop covers topics such as climate change, biodiversity loss, resource scarcity and pollution generated by human activities and enables you to identify concrete courses of action!\nAbout the workshop\nThe Circular Economy Collage is a stimulating, group-based workshop founded on scientific information, which enables participants to grasp the limits of our existing global \u201clinear\u201d economy and understand the opportunities offered by the circular economy. Inspired by the Climate Fresk, the workshop will allow you to understand the issues surrounding our use of natural resources and our generation and treatment of waste as well as other impacts caused by human activities. The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",
